def _busmsg_get(message, key, default=None):
    """Safe getter for both dict payloads and BusMessage/dataclass-like objects."""
    if isinstance(message, dict):
        return _busmsg_get(message, key, default)
    return getattr(message, key, default)
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""X87B Autonomous Worker Dispatcher import fix for AI Local OS."""
from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import importlib.util
import json
import os
import sys
import time
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

def _resolve_aios_root() -> Path:
    explicit = os._busmsg_get(environ, "AI_LOCAL_OS_ROOT") or os._busmsg_get(environ, "AIOS_ROOT")
    if explicit:
        return Path(explicit)

    candidates = [
        Path("/app"),
        Path(r"D:\\openwebui"),
        Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent,
    ]

    for candidate in candidates:
        try:
            if (candidate / "core" / "x86_agent_bus.py").exists():
                return candidate
        except Exception:
            pass

    return Path(r"D:\\openwebui")


ROOT = _resolve_aios_root()
CORE_DIR = ROOT / "core"
RUNTIME_DIR = ROOT / "runtime"
TEMP_DIR = RUNTIME_DIR / "temp"
BUS_DIR = RUNTIME_DIR / "x86_agent_bus"
MESSAGES_DIR = BUS_DIR / "messages"
REPORT_DIR = RUNTIME_DIR / "reports"
STATE_DIR = RUNTIME_DIR / "x87_worker_dispatcher"
STATE_FILE = STATE_DIR / "state.json"

ROUTE_NEXT = {
    "DEBUG": "PATCHER",
    "PATCHER": "VERIFY",
    "VERIFY": "REPORT",
}


def utc_stamp() -> str:
    return time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())


def now_ms() -> int:
    return int(time.time() * 1000)


def safe_write_json(path: Path, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    tmp = path.with_suffix(path.suffix + ".tmp")
    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(data, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    tmp.replace(path)


def load_json(path: Path, default: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    if not path.exists():
        return default
    try:
        return json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    except Exception as exc:
        return {**default, "load_warning": f"Failed to load {path}: {exc}"}


def load_x86_bus_class():
    bus_file = CORE_DIR / "x86_agent_bus.py"
    if not bus_file.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"X86 dependency missing: {bus_file}")

    module_name = "x86_agent_bus_runtime"
    spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(module_name, str(bus_file))
    if spec is None or spec.loader is None:
        raise RuntimeError(f"Cannot import X86 bus from {bus_file}")

    module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)

    # X87B root-cause fix:
    # Python 3.13 dataclasses expect cls.__module__ to exist in sys.modules
    # while decorators execute during exec_module().
    sys.modules[module_name] = module

    spec.loader.exec_module(module)
    return module.AgentBus


# X97E7_BUSMESSAGE_INPUT_NORMALIZATION
def _x97e7_busmessage_to_dict(msg):
    """Normalize x86 BusMessage/dataclass objects to dict before dispatcher .get(...) access."""
    if isinstance(msg, dict):
        return msg
    try:
        from dataclasses import asdict, is_dataclass
        if is_dataclass(msg):
            return asdict(msg)
    except Exception:
        pass
    data = {}
    for key in ("id", "ts", "from_role", "to_role", "task", "payload", "status"):
        try:
            if hasattr(msg, key):
                data[key] = getattr(msg, key)
        except Exception:
            pass
    if data:
        data.setdefault("_x97e7_normalized_from", type(msg).__name__)
        return data
    return {"_x97e7_normalize_error": f"unsupported message type: {type(msg).__name__}"}

class WorkerDispatcher:

    # X97B2_PLANNER_DRIVEN_RUNTIME_DISPATCH
    def _x97b2_get_x96_plan(self, task_obj):
        """Return x96_plan dict from common task/message shapes without breaking fallback."""
        if not isinstance(task_obj, dict):
            return None
        direct = _busmsg_get(task_obj, "x96_plan")
        if isinstance(direct, dict):
            return direct
        payload = _busmsg_get(task_obj, "payload")
        if isinstance(payload, dict):
            nested = _busmsg_get(payload, "x96_plan")
            if isinstance(nested, dict):
                return nested
        meta = _busmsg_get(task_obj, "metadata")
        if isinstance(meta, dict):
            nested = _busmsg_get(meta, "x96_plan")
            if isinstance(nested, dict):
                return nested
        return None

    def _x97b2_extract_role(self, step):
        """Accept role fields used by planner variants."""
        if not isinstance(step, dict):
            return None
        for key in ("role", "to_role", "worker_role", "agent_role", "name"):
            val = _busmsg_get(step, key)
            if isinstance(val, str) and val.strip():
                return val.strip().upper()
        return None

    def _x97b2_resolve_next_role(self, task_obj, current_role, result):
        """Plan-first next-role resolver; ROUTE_NEXT remains safety fallback."""
        fallback = _busmsg_get(ROUTE_NEXT, current_role)
        try:
            plan = self._x97b2_get_x96_plan(task_obj)
            if not isinstance(plan, dict):
                return fallback
            steps = _busmsg_get(plan, "steps")
            if not isinstance(steps, list) or not steps:
                return fallback

            cur = current_role.upper() if isinstance(current_role, str) else current_role
            current_index = None
            for idx, step in enumerate(steps):
                role = self._x97b2_extract_role(step)
                if role == cur:
                    current_index = idx
                    if isinstance(step, dict):
                        step["status"] = "done" if isinstance(result, dict) and _busmsg_get(result, "ok") else "failed"
                        step["last_result_ok"] = bool(isinstance(result, dict) and _busmsg_get(result, "ok"))
                        step["retries"] = int(_busmsg_get(step, "retries") or 0)
                    break

            if current_index is None:
                return fallback

            for next_step in steps[current_index + 1:]:
                next_role = self._x97b2_extract_role(next_step)
                if next_role:
                    if isinstance(next_step, dict) and not _busmsg_get(next_step, "status"):
                        next_step["status"] = "queued"
                    plan["x97b2_runtime_dispatch"] = "planner_driven"
                    return next_role

            plan["x97b2_runtime_dispatch"] = "planner_complete"
            return None
        except Exception as exc:
            try:
                if isinstance(task_obj, dict):
                    task_obj.setdefault("x97b2_dispatch_error", str(exc))
            except Exception:
                pass
            return fallback

    def __init__(self) -> None:
        STATE_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        REPORT_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        AgentBus = load_x86_bus_class()
        self.bus = AgentBus()
        self.state = load_json(STATE_FILE, {
            "release": "X87B_WORKER_DISPATCHER_IMPORTFIX",
            "created_at": utc_stamp(),
            "cycles": 0,
            "processed_total": 0,
            "last_cycle": None,
            "last_error": None,
        })

    def save(self) -> None:
        safe_write_json(STATE_FILE, self.state)

    def handle_message(self, msg: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        # X97E7: BusMessage/dataclass may come directly from x86 send(); convert before msg.get(...).

        msg = _x97e7_busmessage_to_dict(msg)
        to_role = str(_busmsg_get(msg, "to_role", "")).upper()
        task = str(_busmsg_get(msg, "task", ""))
        payload = _busmsg_get(msg, "payload") if isinstance(_busmsg_get(msg, "payload"), dict) else {}

        result = {
            "message_id": _busmsg_get(msg, "id"),
            "role": to_role,
            "task": task,
            "input_payload": payload,
            "handled_at": utc_stamp(),
            "ok": True,
            "summary": "",
            "routed_to": None,
        }

        if to_role == "DEBUG":
            result["summary"] = "DEBUG worker consumed evidence and confirmed root-cause-first handoff."
            result["output_payload"] = {
                "root_cause": _busmsg_get(payload, "root_cause") or "pending_real_log_review",
                "evidence": _busmsg_get(payload, "evidence") or payload,
                "source_message": _busmsg_get(msg, "id"),
            }
        elif to_role == "PATCHER":
            result["summary"] = "PATCHER worker consumed confirmed cause/artifact context."
            result["output_payload"] = {
                "artifact": _busmsg_get(payload, "artifact") or r"D:\openwebui\_patch_inbox",
                "patch_rule": "target confirmed cause only",
                "source_message": _busmsg_get(msg, "id"),
            }
        elif to_role == "VERIFY":
            result["summary"] = "VERIFY worker consumed artifact and produced verify handoff."
            result["output_payload"] = {
                "verify": _busmsg_get(payload, "verify") or "pending_x75_check",
                "source_message": _busmsg_get(msg, "id"),
            }
        elif to_role == "REPORT":
            result["summary"] = "REPORT worker consumed final verification payload."
            result["output_payload"] = {
                "final": payload,
                "source_message": _busmsg_get(msg, "id"),
            }
        else:
            result["ok"] = False
            result["summary"] = f"No worker handler for role {to_role}"
            result["output_payload"] = {"source_message": _busmsg_get(msg, "id")}

        # X97E_PLANNER_SEED_AND_PAYLOAD_PROPAGATION: carry plan metadata from input payload into routing context
        x97e_plan_context = None
        try:
            x97e_input_payload = _busmsg_get(msg, "payload") if isinstance(msg, dict) else None
            if isinstance(x97e_input_payload, dict):
                x97e_plan_context = _busmsg_get(x97e_input_payload, "x96_plan")
            if x97e_plan_context and isinstance(_busmsg_get(result, "output_payload"), dict):
                result["output_payload"].setdefault("x96_plan", x97e_plan_context)
                result["output_payload"].setdefault("x97e_plan_propagated", True)
        except Exception as exc:
            try:
                result.setdefault("x97e_plan_propagation_error", str(exc))
            except Exception:
                pass
        x97e_task_for_route = {"task": task, "x96_plan": x97e_plan_context} if x97e_plan_context else task
        next_role = self._x97b2_resolve_next_role(x97e_task_for_route, to_role, result)
        if result["ok"] and next_role:
            sent = self.bus.send(to_role, next_role, task, result["output_payload"])
            result["routed_to"] = next_role
            result["routed_message_id"] = sent.id

        return result

    def cycle(self, roles: Optional[List[str]] = None, limit_per_role: int = 10) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        roles = [r.upper() for r in (roles or ["DEBUG", "PATCHER", "VERIFY", "REPORT"])]
        processed: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []

        for role in roles:
            consumed = self.bus.consume(role, limit=limit_per_role)
            for msg in consumed:
                processed.append(self.handle_message(msg))

        self.state["cycles"] = int(self._busmsg_get(state, "cycles", 0)) + 1
        self.state["processed_total"] = int(self._busmsg_get(state, "processed_total", 0)) + len(processed)
        self.state["last_cycle"] = {
            "ts": utc_stamp(),
            "roles": roles,
            "processed": len(processed),
        }
        self.state["last_error"] = None
        self.save()

        report = {
            "ok": True,
            "release": "X87B_WORKER_DISPATCHER_IMPORTFIX",
            "processed": processed,
            "processed_count": len(processed),
            "state_file": str(STATE_FILE),
        }
        out = REPORT_DIR / f"x87b_worker_dispatcher_report_{now_ms()}.json"
        safe_write_json(out, report)
        report["report_file"] = str(out)
        return report

    # X97E_PLANNER_SEED_AND_PAYLOAD_PROPAGATION: planner-aware first bus message
    def seed(self, task: str, x96_plan=None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Seed the first runtime message.

        Plan-first behavior:
        - if x96_plan.steps[] is valid, queue the first planned role, normally SCOUT
        - attach x96_plan to the first payload so downstream routing can stay planner-driven

        Fallback behavior:
        - if the plan is missing/invalid, keep the historical SCOUT -> DEBUG seed path
        """
        payload = {"finding": "seeded by X87B dispatcher", "evidence": str(TEMP_DIR)}
        from_role = "SCOUT"
        to_role = "DEBUG"
        plan_first_role = None
        try:
            if isinstance(x96_plan, dict):
                steps = _busmsg_get(x96_plan, "steps") or []
                if isinstance(steps, list) and steps:
                    first = steps[0]
                    if isinstance(first, dict):
                        plan_first_role = _busmsg_get(first, "role") or _busmsg_get(first, "to_role") or _busmsg_get(first, "agent_role")
                if plan_first_role:
                    from_role = "SCOUT"
                    to_role = str(plan_first_role).upper()
                    payload["x96_plan"] = x96_plan
                    payload["x97e_seed_mode"] = "planner_first"
                    payload["x97e_first_role"] = to_role
        except Exception as exc:
            payload["x97e_seed_error"] = str(exc)

        sent = self.bus.send(from_role, to_role, task, payload)
        return {"ok": True, "seed_message": _busmsg_get(sent, "id"), "task": task, "seeded_to": to_role, "x97e_seed_mode": _busmsg_get(payload, "x97e_seed_mode", "fallback_route_next")}

    def demo(self, task: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        seed = self.seed(task)
        cycles = []
        for _ in range(4):
            cycles.append(self.cycle(limit_per_role=20))
        report = {
            "ok": True,
            "release": "X87B_WORKER_DISPATCHER_IMPORTFIX",
            "task": task,
            "seed": seed,
            "cycles": cycles,
            "state_file": str(STATE_FILE),
        }
        out = REPORT_DIR / f"x87b_worker_dispatcher_demo_{now_ms()}.json"
        safe_write_json(out, report)
        report["report_file"] = str(out)
        return report

    def status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "ok": True,
            "release": "X87B_WORKER_DISPATCHER_IMPORTFIX",
            "state_file": str(STATE_FILE),
            "state": self.state,
            "x86_messages_dir": str(MESSAGES_DIR),
            "x86_exists": (CORE_DIR / "x86_agent_bus.py").exists(),
            "import_fix": "sys.modules[module_name] registered before exec_module",
        }


def cli() -> int:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="X87B autonomous worker dispatcher importfix")
    sub = parser.add_subparsers(dest="cmd")

    p_seed = sub.add_parser("seed")
    p_seed.add_argument("--task", default="x87b seeded task")

    p_cycle = sub.add_parser("cycle")
    p_cycle.add_argument("--roles", default="DEBUG,PATCHER,VERIFY,REPORT")
    p_cycle.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=10)

    p_demo = sub.add_parser("demo")
    p_demo.add_argument("--task", default="x87b dispatcher smoke")

    sub.add_parser("status")

    args = parser.parse_args()
    dispatcher = WorkerDispatcher()

    if args.cmd == "seed":
        print(json.dumps(dispatcher.seed(args.task), ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
        return 0

    if args.cmd == "cycle":
        roles = [x.strip() for x in args.roles.split(",") if x.strip()]
        print(json.dumps(dispatcher.cycle(roles=roles, limit_per_role=args.limit), ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
        return 0

    if args.cmd == "demo":
        print(json.dumps(dispatcher.demo(args.task), ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
        return 0

    if args.cmd == "status":
        print(json.dumps(dispatcher.status(), ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
        return 0

    parser.print_help()
    return 2


if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(cli())




=== x86 bus ===
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""X86 Inter-Agent Task Bus for AI Local OS."""
from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import json
import os
import time
import uuid
from dataclasses import asdict, dataclass
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

ROOT = Path(os.environ.get("AI_LOCAL_OS_ROOT", r"D:\openwebui"))
RUNTIME_DIR = ROOT / "runtime"
BUS_DIR = RUNTIME_DIR / "x86_agent_bus"
MESSAGES_DIR = BUS_DIR / "messages"
REPORT_DIR = RUNTIME_DIR / "reports"
STATE_FILE = BUS_DIR / "state.json"

ROLES = ("SCOUT", "DEBUG", "PATCHER", "VERIFY", "REPORT")
ALLOWED_TRANSITIONS = {
    "SCOUT": ["SCOUT", "DEBUG", "REPORT"],  # X97C2 allows planner seed into SCOUT
    "DEBUG": ["PATCHER", "VERIFY", "REPORT"],
    "PATCHER": ["VERIFY", "REPORT"],
    "VERIFY": ["REPORT"],
    "REPORT": [],
}


def utc_stamp() -> str:
    return time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())


def now_ms() -> int:
    return int(time.time() * 1000)


def safe_write_json(path: Path, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    tmp = path.with_suffix(path.suffix + ".tmp")
    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(data, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    tmp.replace(path)


def load_json(path: Path, default: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    if not path.exists():
        return default
    try:
        return json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    except Exception as exc:
        return {**default, "load_warning": f"Failed to load {path}: {exc}"}


@dataclass
class BusMessage:
    id: str
    ts: str
    from_role: str
    to_role: str
    task: str
    payload: Dict[str, Any]
    status: str = "queued"


class AgentBus:
    def __init__(self) -> None:
        BUS_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        MESSAGES_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        REPORT_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        self.state = load_json(STATE_FILE, {
            "release": "X86_AGENT_BUS",
            "created_at": utc_stamp(),
            "messages_total": 0,
            "last_message": None,
            "last_error": None,
        })

    def save(self) -> None:
        safe_write_json(STATE_FILE, self.state)

    def message_path(self, message_id: str) -> Path:
        return MESSAGES_DIR / f"{message_id}.json"

    def validate_role(self, role: str) -> str:
        role = role.upper().strip()
        if role not in ROLES:
            raise ValueError(f"invalid role {role}; allowed={', '.join(ROLES)}")
        return role

    def validate_transition(self, from_role: str, to_role: str) -> None:
        allowed = ALLOWED_TRANSITIONS.get(from_role, [])
        if to_role not in allowed:
            raise ValueError(f"invalid transition {from_role}->{to_role}; allowed={allowed}")

    def send(self, from_role: str, to_role: str, task: str, payload: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None) -> BusMessage:
        from_role = self.validate_role(from_role)
        to_role = self.validate_role(to_role)
        self.validate_transition(from_role, to_role)
        message = BusMessage(
            id=f"x86_{now_ms()}_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            ts=utc_stamp(),
            from_role=from_role,
            to_role=to_role,
            task=task,
            payload=payload or {},
        )
        data = asdict(message)
        safe_write_json(self.message_path(message.id), data)
        self.state["messages_total"] = int(self.state.get("messages_total", 0)) + 1
        self.state["last_message"] = data
        self.state["last_error"] = None
        self.save()
        return message

    def list_messages(self, status: Optional[str] = None) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        rows = []
        for path in sorted(MESSAGES_DIR.glob("*.json"), key=lambda p: p.stat().st_mtime):
            item = load_json(path, {})
            if status and item.get("status") != status:
                continue
            rows.append(item)
        return rows

    def consume(self, role: str, limit: int = 10) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        role = self.validate_role(role)
        consumed = []
        for item in self.list_messages(status="queued"):
            if item.get("to_role") != role:
                continue
            item["status"] = "consumed"
            item["consumed_at"] = utc_stamp()
            safe_write_json(self.message_path(item["id"]), item)
            consumed.append(item)
            if len(consumed) >= limit:
                break
        self.state["last_consume"] = {"role": role, "count": len(consumed), "ts": utc_stamp()}
        self.save()
        return consumed

    def demo_chain(self, task: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        sent = []
        sent.append(asdict(self.send("SCOUT", "DEBUG", task, {"finding": "project/context collected"})))
        sent.append(asdict(self.send("DEBUG", "PATCHER", task, {"root_cause": "confirmed by real log", "evidence": "runtime/temp/*.txt"})))
        sent.append(asdict(self.send("PATCHER", "VERIFY", task, {"artifact": r"D:\openwebui\_patch_inbox\x86_agent_bus"})))
        sent.append(asdict(self.send("VERIFY", "REPORT", task, {"verify": "pass"})))
        report = {
            "ok": True,
            "release": "X86_AGENT_BUS",
            "task": task,
            "sent": sent,
            "state_file": str(STATE_FILE),
            "messages_dir": str(MESSAGES_DIR),
        }
        out = REPORT_DIR / f"x86_agent_bus_report_{now_ms()}.json"
        safe_write_json(out, report)
        report["report_file"] = str(out)
        return report

    def status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        messages = self.list_messages()
        return {
            "ok": True,
            "release": "X86_AGENT_BUS",
            "state_file": str(STATE_FILE),
            "messages_dir": str(MESSAGES_DIR),
            "messages_total_files": len(messages),
            "state": self.state,
            "roles": list(ROLES),
            "transitions": ALLOWED_TRANSITIONS,
        }


def parse_payload(raw: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    if not raw:
        return {}
    try:
        data = json.loads(raw)
        if not isinstance(data, dict):
            raise ValueError("payload JSON must be object")
        return data
    except Exception as exc:
        raise SystemExit(f"invalid --payload JSON: {exc}")


def cli() -> int:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="X86 inter-agent task bus")
    sub = parser.add_subparsers(dest="cmd")

    p_send = sub.add_parser("send")
    p_send.add_argument("--from-role", required=True)
    p_send.add_argument("--to-role", required=True)
    p_send.add_argument("--task", required=True)
    p_send.add_argument("--payload", default="{}")

    p_consume = sub.add_parser("consume")
    p_consume.add_argument("--role", required=True)
    p_consume.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=10)

    p_list = sub.add_parser("list")
    p_list.add_argument("--status", default=None)

    p_demo = sub.add_parser("demo-chain")
    p_demo.add_argument("--task", default="x86 bus smoke")

    sub.add_parser("status")

    args = parser.parse_args()
    bus = AgentBus()

    if args.cmd == "send":
        msg = bus.send(args.from_role, args.to_role, args.task, parse_payload(args.payload))
        print(json.dumps({"ok": True, "message": asdict(msg)}, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
        return 0

    if args.cmd == "consume":
        rows = bus.consume(args.role, args.limit)
        print(json.dumps({"ok": True, "role": args.role.upper(), "count": len(rows), "messages": rows}, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
        return 0

    if args.cmd == "list":
        rows = bus.list_messages(args.status)
        print(json.dumps({"ok": True, "count": len(rows), "messages": rows}, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
        return 0

    if args.cmd == "demo-chain":
        report = bus.demo_chain(args.task)
        print(json.dumps(report, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
        return 0

    if args.cmd == "status":
        print(json.dumps(bus.status(), ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
        return 0

    parser.print_help()
    return 2
